- **Technical analysis (blofin_technical_analysis, 1H, 100 bars)**:

- No funding rate, order‑book depth, or news fetched yet.

Constraints (Profit Doctrine):
- Target 5‑10 % move, R:R ≥ 4:1 (prefer 5:1).
- Tight stop ~1 % above entry for losers; large TP for winners.
- Veto if flat/choppy or R:R < 4:1.

Open items / next actions (still within Loop 1):
1. Call **blofin_get_funding_rate** for TAC‑USDT to assess crowding bias (funding_bias).
2. Call **blofin_get_order_book** (size 20) for depth/imbalance.
3. Call **blofin_get_candles** (optional higher‑timeframe, e.g., 4H) to confirm support/resistance.

Proceed with steps 1‑5, then synthesize JSON. End of Loop 1.

- H2: WLD‑USDT is overbought and may reverse, offering a short asymmetric downside.  
- H3: The market is flat/choppy, so veto the trade.  

**3. Evaluate and Choose**  
To decide we need live data: current price, recent volatility, EMA/RSI, funding rate, order‑book imbalance, and any news catalysts. I will gather these sequentially, respecting rate limits.

**4. Act and Update Memory** – Call the required tools.

1. **Ticker** for price and 24h stats.

}

**5. Reflect**  
These calls will give a complete picture of price action, momentum, volatility, funding pressure, order‑book skew, and any macro news. Once results return, I will compute:

- **move_potential_pct**: distance from current price to the nearest strong support/resistance (or Bollinger band) expressed as a percent, checking that a 5‑10 % move is feasible.  
- **technical_score**: combine TA scores (EMA crossover, RSI, momentum).  
- **funding_bias**: from funding rate (positive = long bias, negative = short).  
- **key_levels**: recent support/resistance, pivot, Bollinger bands.  
- **confidence**: weighted blend of technical_score, funding_bias, order‑book imbalance, news sentiment.  
- **veto**: true if R:R < 4:1 (stop‑loss at ~1 % and TP < 4 % away) or market is flat.  
- **thesis**: concise narrative.

After receiving the data I will synthesize the JSON and finish Loop 1.
